  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0f2f76d4-3c5c-44c6-9ad3-49099a1dd95b'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText1800189141380112592" style="display:none">Beautiful new cover. Same beautiful story. <br /><br /><br />What happens when the very thing ruining your life ends up saving it?<br /><br />I was never one to believe in spirits—until six years ago, when a bone-chilling accident changed my life…forever. <br /><br />My name is Charlotte, but most people call me Char…and I have a special gift. <br /><br />I talk to the dead. 	<br /><br />Make no mistake, I can’t summon them. I’m only able to see and speak to the spirits that linger when they’re unable to crossover. They’re somehow weighted to the world with unfinished affairs. And for the last six years, I’ve relentlessly used my gift to help their lost souls.<br /><br />But it’s come at a price. My life is dark. Feeling despondent, I’ve begun to give up. And in helping the dead, I’ve realized I haven’t allowed myself to live. With no money, no place to go, and most importantly… no hope, I’ve decided there is only one option—to end it all.<br /><br />But fate is a funny thing. One minute, I’m about to leap to my death, and the next, I’m saved by Ike McDermott. The strong, striking soldier stopped me from putting an end to my despair. He’s the kind of man that smiles and brightens an entire room. <br /><br />Sweet and gentle.<br /><br />He is my savior.	<br /><br />And he’s dead.<br /><br />We’ve made an agreement. He’ll help me find a place to stay and a new job if I’ll help him with his unfinished business so that he may crossover.<br /><br />Ike’s unfinished matter involves his twin brother, George. George has been falling apart since Ike’s death and Ike has not been able to compel himself to crossover in peace until he knows George will be okay.<br /><br />When I agreed to help, little did I know that I’d fall in love with the charming folks of Bath County, and…Ike and George McDermott. <br /><br />Now, as both brothers own equal parts of my heart, I am faced with a cruel and unfair predicament. In saving George, I must let go of Ike. <br /><br />But how does one let go of half of their heart?</span>
  <a data-text-id="1800189141380112592" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_1232456023" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1232456023" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1232456023?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/24323918-where-one-goes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1232456023" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18235842399550770518"><b>::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 4.5 stars ::: </b><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426979162i/14151991.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>You know how sometimes you read a blurb for a book and just go "Wow! I need to read that!" ? Well, that's exactly what happened to me here. I'm always on the lookout for different books. I love the romance genre, but I especially love when I come across a story that is unlike any other I've read. Check this out...<br/>__________<br/><br/><i>"One minute, I’m about to leap to my death, and the next, I’m saved by a strong, striking soldier. He’s the kind of man that smile</i></span>
  <span id="freeText18235842399550770518" style="display:none"><b>::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 4.5 stars ::: </b><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426979162i/14151991.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You know how sometimes you read a blurb for a book and just go "Wow! I need to read that!" ? Well, that's exactly what happened to me here. I'm always on the lookout for different books. I love the romance genre, but I especially love when I come across a story that is unlike any other I've read. Check this out...<br>__________<br><br><i>"One minute, I’m about to leap to my death, and the next, I’m saved by a strong, striking soldier. He’s the kind of man that smiles and brightens an entire room. Sweet and gentle. He is my savior. And he’s dead. We’ve made an agreement... I’ll help him with his unfinished business so that he may crossover.<br><br>His unfinished matter involves his twin brother... When I agreed to help, little did I know that I’d fall in love... Now, I am faced with a cruel and unfair predicament. In saving one brother, I must let go of the other..."</i><br>__________<br><br>Pretty intriguing, right?<br><br>Before anything, I'm going to clarify two quick things:<br><br>1. Even if you're not fond of love triangles (like me), I think there's still a good chance you'll love this book because it's just not a traditional triangle since one of the guys is literally not alive. Of course, it's quite emotionally complex, but it's not really like there's actually any "choice" between the guys.<br><br>2. Even if you're not into paranormal stuff, I also think there's a good chance you'll enjoy this book. There's no complicated mythology, it's not a "paranormal world", its just literally that this one girl can see souls who are still around. They look totally normal, they're not evil or malicious. There's nothing spooky or creepy or dark about it. The story just feels REAL. It truly does! Again, I really think anyone who loves romance and is just able to be open minded about this, will love it.<br><br>Ok, moving on!<br><br>This was one of those stories that hooked me right from the start. It just immediately captured my attention. It intrigued me, made me care, and the more I read, the more invested I became. I was simultaneously thrilled and impressed with how real this story felt. Big kudos to the author for that!<br><br>Ike, the dead soldier, really stole my heart. I felt for him so strongly. Here he was stuck around but unable to make a difference. Even though he never once regretted his decision to join the military, what was unable to bear was the damage his death was doing to his brother, George. When he came across Charlotte, he saw in her the opportunity to not only help his brother, but also somehow help her too.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“It’s an odd bond. I’m fighting to give her and my brother life, while she’s fighting to help me let go. Somehow we’ve become tethered to one another, even though we both know our time is limited.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Despite the fact that this book has fairly serious and emotional foundation, I loved the way there'd be these hilarious lines throw in here and there that would literally have me laughing out loud!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You can see me?” I shake my head in disbelief.<br><br>She clenches her eyes closed and groans. “You’re dead.” It’s not a question, but more of a statement…<br><br>“You can really see me?” I ask again, convinced I’m going mad.<br><br>“Dead and stupid,” she mumbles. “Obviously I can see and hear you.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Charlotte's connection to the two brothers was very different. While with Ike, their connection came easily and they bonded very strongly early on, George had a lot of issues to work through before his relationship with Char was able to develop all the way so they had quite an interesting hot/cold dynamic.<br><br>Charlotte and Ike had the ultimate forbidden romance. They both knew they had no chance at any real future, but their emotional connection was no less strong. It was both beautiful and heart-breaking.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Would you dance with me tonight if you could?”<br><br>His brows rise, surprised by my question. Standing, he looks down at me, his expression serious. “Every fucking song.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>You'll see the way it all works out in the end, but I'll say that I thought it all was very beautifully portrayed. I teared up several times -- especially in that dog tag scene! OMG! -- and really felt strongly for each of the characters in their own way... This was just one of those books that I loved everything about.<br><br>If you're a fan of romance and are looking for something different with wonderful writing and really deep emotions, but balanced out with fun humor, and a very unique story then give this book a shot!!<br><br><b>Rating: 4.5 stars. Standalone with paranormal elements. </b><br>_______________________________________<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com/subscribe/" rel="nofollow noopener">Subscribe by email</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="18235842399550770518" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1232416647" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer12687635676600829048"><b>”He saved me so I could save you, which in a way means, you saved me too.”</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>Awwww I really enjoyed this story! I loved all the characters and even though it’s a love triangle it’s pretty obvious how things will end since one of the three is dead. Charlotte’s been a drifter for over five years and her gift and her loneliness have taken its toll. She decides to end her life of servitude and find some relief for her loneliness.<br/><br/><b>"This isn’t a life – it’s a nightmare. A never-ending torment</b></span>
  <span id="freeText12687635676600829048" style="display:none"><b>”He saved me so I could save you, which in a way means, you saved me too.”</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Awwww I really enjoyed this story! I loved all the characters and even though it’s a love triangle it’s pretty obvious how things will end since one of the three is dead. Charlotte’s been a drifter for over five years and her gift and her loneliness have taken its toll. She decides to end her life of servitude and find some relief for her loneliness.<br><br><b>"This isn’t a life – it’s a nightmare. A never-ending torment of death and servitude. And the pain has become too much to bear.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492428367ra/22515641.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Charlotte’s life is saved when she makes a deal with a beautiful fallen solider named Ike.<br><br><b>”What if we make a deal?”<br> <br>“A deal?”<br> <br>“I’ll introduce you to some nice people, help you get a job, a place to stay, and you… you can help me settle things.”</b><br><br>Ike helps Charlotte get set up with a place to stay and a job working for his brother at their once shared restaurant. Ike’s brother, George has been sleeping around with a woman who is also his drug dealer. George is lost amidst his despair over his twin brother’s death.<br><br><b>”Every time I look into your sad, brown eyes, I see my own despair staring back at me.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492428367ra/22515637.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Charlotte develops a relationship with both brothers although one is dead. Her love for both and her abilities not only help the brother’s heal but their family as well. <br> <br><b>”I want so badly for George to be better, to be happy, but his happiness involves him having something I would sell my soul to have.” </b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Ike and Charlotte’s relationship was extremely well done and will get some friend’s eyes teary. I fell completely in LOVE with Ike he was just amazing.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400352957ra/9665873.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>” This is it. This is all there is for us.”</b><br><br>Overall, I was glued to this story and loved all the characters and would definitely recommend friends picking it up! It’s not an angsty story just beautiful one! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492428367ra/22515639.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>”I’ll love her for both of us, Ike,” I whispered.”<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492428367i/22515638.gif" width="390" height="20" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br></b></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1232808885" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1232808885" />
    <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna"><img alt="✦❋Arianna✦❋" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420671997p2/23370948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1232808885?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✦❋Arianna✦❋" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna">✦❋Arianna✦❋</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781311022677" href="/book/show/24890039-where-one-goes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23370948-arianna?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1232808885" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18153633682274248384"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427638505i/14299642.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>What a beautiful story! <i>“Where One Goes”</i> was like nothing I’ve read so far. It’s an emotional story about life, love, loss and moving on. It rarely happens to come across a PNR as touching as this one. I loved everything about it, from the flawless writing to the three endearing main characters. I was so engrossed in this story from the beginning I couldn’t put it down. <br/><br/><i>“Where One Goes”</i> tells the story of Charlotte ‘Char’ Acres a woman who has a special ability since she almost died six years a</span>
  <span id="freeText18153633682274248384" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427638505i/14299642.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>What a beautiful story! <i>“Where One Goes”</i> was like nothing I’ve read so far. It’s an emotional story about life, love, loss and moving on. It rarely happens to come across a PNR as touching as this one. I loved everything about it, from the flawless writing to the three endearing main characters. I was so engrossed in this story from the beginning I couldn’t put it down. <br><br><i>“Where One Goes”</i> tells the story of Charlotte ‘Char’ Acres a woman who has a special ability since she almost died six years ago – she can see and talk with the dead, helping them to resolve their unfinished business. She’s not happy with this unusual ‘gift’, she never asked for it. This ‘gift’ destroyed her life, has cost her any semblance of normalcy. Because of this ‘gift’ she lost her family and her friends. Charlotte lost her hope as well. She’s lonely and all she wants is everything to end. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"This isn’t a life—it’s a nightmare. A never-ending torment of death and servitude. And the pain has become too much to bear."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Charlotte is ‘save’ by Ike, a fallen soldier who makes her an offer – she will help him resolve his unfinished business and he will help her finding her a place to stay and a job. Ike’s ‘unfinished business’ is his twin George who feels lost, struggling with the loss of his brother. On top of that, George’s fuck buddy is a woman who gives him drugs destroying him more and more every day. Ike helps Charlotte getting a job as a waitress at George’s restaurant and 'finds' her a place to stay. <br><br>Charlotte finds herself drawn to Ike. Time passes, they get to know each other better and she realizes that she wants more with him. She knows it’s going to hurt when Ike has to leave. Ike is drawn to Charlotte as well – to her beauty and to her personality. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It’s only been two days since I found her on the bridge and already I feel tied to her, like she’s a part of me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>George’s life shattered when he found out his twin died in Afghanistan. He’s using drugs and he’s in a relationship with a woman who belongs to someone else. He’s ashamed, but he only wants to forget. He can tell his new waitress is something else entirely. She’s not only beautiful, but she has a great character as well. He tries to fight this attraction, especially when he realizes Charlotte wants to help him getting better. He thinks he doesn’t need a woman to save him. <br><br>If at first Charlotte finds herself drawn only to Ike, so he realizes she’s drawn to George as well. They are similar, but at the same time they are different from each other. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427638505i/14299643.jpg" width="400" height="448" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“How do I save him, and let you go at the same time? How do I do that?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Charlotte finds in both men and in the small town of Warm Springs what she has looking for all this time – peace, hope and love. Ike falls in love with Charlotte, but he knows he can’t have her. He also knows she feels something for his brother, that she is carefree and fun with him and that they could help each other.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“...and I know I love her because letting her go will be one of the hardest things I’ll ever have to do, but I’ll do it gladly knowing she’s safe and happy.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This was such an emotional read! Like I mentioned above I loved everything about this novel. The three main characters were so endearing. While I loved them all, Ike was my favorite character. I absolutely loved him! He was such an amazing man. My heart ached for him from the beginning. At times I wanted so badly to hug him. His love for Charlotte is so pure and genuine and I really felt it. It was a beautiful thing to ‘see; and ‘feel’. He loves her so fiercely. *sigh* <br><br>At times he took my breath away and not only with his words. He has such a big heart, he was and he still is a good son and brother. He loves George dearly and all he wants is to see him healed, to see that he’s ready to move on, that he feels and lives like he used to. Even if he knows it’s not possible to be with Charlotte, he just wants her to be happy and if his twin is the man for her, he is content and happy for them . I must admit there were times I wanted Charlotte to end up with him. I knew like everyone else it’s not possible, but I wanted it so much. Charlotte was a great heroine. She’s kind-hearted, compassionate, strong and feisty and I really, really liked her. I loved her interactions with both brothers and how their relationships progressed. And I really felt her love for both of them. I also understood her love for both of them, especially since she loves them in different ways. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Charlotte . . . I want you. All of you. The good, the bad, and the ugly. I love you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>My heart also broke for George. He is a lost soul. He lost his way when his twin died. He knows he’s selfish doing drugs and that he’s a liar and he’s ashamed of himself. For the first time in almost ten months he feels alive. Charlotte makes him feel and gives him hope and I loved for that. Even if he’s an as* at times he loves Charlotte with all his heart. He also understands (in some way) her relationship with his dead brother. And I liked that about him.<br><br>While I knew from the beginning how everything will end I found the story addictive and the storyline interesting. <br><br>All in all, <i>“When One Goes”</i> was a beautiful, emotional, refreshing story that will certainly touch your heart, with lovable characters, interesting storyline and great writing. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427638549i/14299649.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="18153633682274248384" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1234180350" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1234180350" />
    <a title="Brandi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi"><img alt="Brandi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1384348451p2/5494655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1234180350?book_show_action=true">Mar 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi">Brandi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/24323918-where-one-goes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1234180350" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer806066151354446415"><br/><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427221007i/14250202._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I absolutely adored this story. <i>Where One Goes</i> is a unique story about love, loss and moving on. The main character, Charlotte, can communicate with the dead, and while this plays a big part in the story, its not campy and honestly I wouldn't even label it as paranormal, I would say its spiritual. Charlotte has spent years wandering, alone, moving from place to place. Her parents think she's nuts and the last 6 years have done a number on her, she is tired of being lonely and surrounded</span>
  <span id="freeText806066151354446415" style="display:none"><br><b>4.5 Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427221007i/14250202._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I absolutely adored this story. <i>Where One Goes</i> is a unique story about love, loss and moving on. The main character, Charlotte, can communicate with the dead, and while this plays a big part in the story, its not campy and honestly I wouldn't even label it as paranormal, I would say its spiritual. Charlotte has spent years wandering, alone, moving from place to place. Her parents think she's nuts and the last 6 years have done a number on her, she is tired of being lonely and surrounded by death.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427220437i/14250091.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>While Char may be struggling with her gift, the dead who encounter her are grateful, being able to communicate with her, helps them resolve unfinished business that has kept them from moving on. On the day she plans to end it all, she meets a fallen solider, Ike, who makes her an offer she is unable to refuse.<br><br><i>
  <b>"I'll introduce you to some nice people, help you get a job, a place to stay, and you...you can help me settle things."</b>
</i><br><br>Ike needs Charlotte to help his family, they are all struggling with the loss, especially his twin brother, George. So Charlotte finds herself in Ike's hometown, and while spending time with the brothers, also finds herself falling in love. <br><br><i>
  <b>I shouldn’t be reacting this way to him. I’m only meant to help him crossover…I mean, what kind of person develops a crush on a set of brothers, let alone with a dead one in the mix? </b>
</i><br><br>This was truly a beautiful story, that had me in tears a few times. I loved these characters, and it was probably one of the most heartbreaking love triangles. A story filled with heart, humor and hope, I loved every word. <br><br><i>
  <b>"You weren't given a choice, Charlotte. The choice is already made."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427218268i/14249702.jpg" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="806066151354446415" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1246340702" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1246340702" />
    <a title="Snow" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31719636-snow"><img alt="Snow" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465808156p2/31719636.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1246340702?book_show_action=true">Apr 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Snow" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Snow" href="/user/show/31719636-snow">Snow</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/24323918-where-one-goes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=5-star-read">5-star-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=funny">funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=ugly-cry">ugly-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=best-ever">best-ever</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1246340702" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1655428029578029088"><b>6 "this-messed-me-up-in-a-good-way" stars</b><br/><br/>This is gonna be the longest review I’ve ever written cause there are no simple words to say how I feel and I’m sure I’m gonna miss something after I’m done…<br/><br/>This was an unusual choice for me and it was recommended to me by my dearest friend <b>ANA</b> cause I was in a totally overdrived state of mind LOL and she offered a way out of it. I didn’t read it then. <br/><br/>The first thought after reading the blurb was: the hell is this? She falls in love with the ghost? Damn,</span>
  <span id="freeText1655428029578029088" style="display:none"><b>6 "this-messed-me-up-in-a-good-way" stars</b><br><br>This is gonna be the longest review I’ve ever written cause there are no simple words to say how I feel and I’m sure I’m gonna miss something after I’m done…<br><br>This was an unusual choice for me and it was recommended to me by my dearest friend <b>ANA</b> cause I was in a totally overdrived state of mind LOL and she offered a way out of it. I didn’t read it then. <br><br>The first thought after reading the blurb was: the hell is this? She falls in love with the ghost? Damn, I’m not in a mood for that. <br>And I’ve put it on hold for a while.<br><br>Don’t get me wrong, I will read anything that stirs my interest, but to be honest this book was not it at that time.<br><br>Then my friend <b>Kathleen</b> said I should read it…and I was still like...nah<br>You see, if there’s a lot of crying involved, I tend to roll my eyes in annoyance and I'm a bit sceptical about the whole thing getting this itchy feeling that it's gonna turn into a mushy pile of smth mushy...yikes and that never works for me!<br><br><b>
  <i>I didn't expect this amount of "feels" from this storyline and I certainly wasn't prepared for that. LOL So, when i finally dived in, I had to brace myself for an emotional breakdown...(and that's fuckin first for me!)</i>
</b><br><br><b>And here we go, right down to it! THIS BOOK changed me!<br>It made me question my own beliefs about love, about completion, about second chances, about the belief itself.</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>It made me laugh.<br>It made me think and re-think.<br>It made me dream.<br>It made me sad.<br>It made me hopeful and yes,<br>It made me cry.</i>
</blockquote><br>In short, <b>Charlotte</b> is a young woman who has a gift of seeing and hearing the dead and has been “helping” them to crossover for the past six year after she lived through her own tragic experience BUT now she’s drained and tired of being lonely, empty and broke and decides to end it all. In the last moment she’s saved by none other than a ghost. A Soldier named Ike. He makes her a deal. He’ll help her to build herself up again if she helps him with his brother George who’s having a difficult time in coping with the death of his sibling.<br><br>And the story further unravels an unexpected journey as for our characters and the readers, you do not expect the rise of the emotional high in such an intensity as one does…<br><br><b>
  <i>NOTE: No, there are no actual answers given here about the death and the meaning of religious beliefs or impacts, you won’t find it here…this scenery is set to develop a notion of what is possible to feel and to acknowledge as possible in the first place in dealing with the emotions in quantity and variety of them</i>
</b><br><i>
  <blockquote>"The brothers are so different, polar opposites in fact, that I find myself drawn to each one for different reasons. One is so strong and responsible; so much so, not even death can keep him from taking care of those he loves. The other, broken and lost, wishing time could rewind on one hand, but using any method necessary to forget time on the other.<br><br>In Ike, I crave his warmth and good heart. In George, I crave his likeness, the understanding we share."</blockquote>
</i><br>About the heroine – <u>Charlotte/Char</u> – <b>never had I encounter a heroine that made me happy she existed, she could be a role model on how to deal with loss, how to raise yourself from bottom and take the life by the balls…accepting her own flaws, making the most of it on an everyday basis, making herself open and accessible to new feelings, impossible feelings, that can never be true and grow with them…<br><br>dealing with hardship with snarky humor and positive thinking…just wow, I bow to you!</b><br><br>I’m not into triangles, or multiple relationships or other messed up connections people get themselves into BUT I do believe that we can and that it is possible to love more than one person in our lives and that we do get to expand our hearts to that notion, we know of motherly love, lover’s love, friend’s love, <b>
  <i>love is not the one that should be labeled at all…it should be given in full without exceptions, without regrets BUT it should not be handled lightly or be used in order to hurt…so yes I’m expanding my heart toward that notion</i>
</b><br><br>And this story was so much more…it was a <b>non-physical love that brought the kindered spirits and souls to know each other on a higher, pure level of existence. It’s the story of how to keep on going, keep on surviving, <u>keep on living and not just existing</u></b><br><br>I fell in love with both male characters, <b>(Ike) and (George)</b>…but I fell for the notion of what they represented. They represented <b>
  <i>HOPE, PEACE, COMPLETION</i>
</b> of being whole, being ready to live up to your own expectations, desires, wishes, dreams, being the human in full intensity of the word, <b>being the SOUL that DOESN’T expire with the physical dead line…</b><br><br>My heart broke for <b>Ike</b> – a young life taken away too soon from his loved ones, <b>
  <i>he represented the unfairness of life and the second chance in comprehension of it</i>
</b>, of making the most of the notion of what could have been, of what ifs and <u>
  <b>not regretting the misfortune of the situation of the fact that the life was not an option BUT what remained was the hope, hope of fulfillment through out the ones that are alive</b>
</u>…<br><br>My heart, once more, broke for <b>George</b> – the man who was <b>lost and wounded, who existed in the shadows of his physical shell BUT didn’t live</b>…<br><b>he found redemption, he found forgivness, he found a second chance, he found love and was saved by the notion that things DO NOT end with death. They are meant to be apart so one can mend it and make it whole again, NEVER the same BUT different whole.</b><br><br><b>Cause it’s not about the <i>death</i> per se, as death is a part of life, it’s <i>the living</i> that is hard, those who are left behind are supposed to move on, grow and make themselves whole over and over again…dying is the easy part!</b><br><br>This is the first book that had secondary characters that were as equally important to me as the main ones – <b>Sniper</b> (large, pierced, stud of a man, ex-military who warmed my heart with his loyalty, snarky lines and big heart of his own); <b>Anna</b> (perky blonde who’s warmth and openness made Charlotte welcomed without hesitation); <b>Mr and Mrs Mercer</b> (an old couple who lost their daughter, good doers who take Char under their wings); <b>Ike and George’s family</b>, especially <b>Cameron</b>, the youngest brother (boy, he made me laugh on several occasions)…<br><br><b>This book made me <i>grow</i> in so many ways and it will stay with me for a long time…</b><br><br>it made me <b>laugh…</b><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“How the hell did you cut your ass, but not your hands or knees?”<br>“I’m talented in the arts of clumsiness. I’m a sensei, really,” she retorts and he chuckles.<br>“I think you’re going to have to pull these down, Charlotte.”<br>“No fucking way!” she almost shrieks as she straightens to a stand. “I’m not putting my bare ass in your face, George.”<br>“I can’t see the full cut.” George leans back, fighting the grin that wants to break out across his face. “You’re going to have to pull them down.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>It made me <b>swoon…</b><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I asked you to dance because like every other guy here, I want to dance with the most beautiful woman in the room.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>It made me <b>more perceptive…bolder</b><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“But you’ve seen more of me than anyone has in a long time. All the ugly parts. Things I’m not proud of.”<br>“I want to know all of you, too. The good, the bad, and the ugly.”<br>“You should go home, Charlotte,” he moans in pain. “I don’t want you to see me like this.”<br>Taking his hand in mine, I kiss it. “I’m not going anywhere. The good, the bad, and the ugly . . . remember?”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Made me <b>hopeful…and open to new aspects…</b><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“So to answer your question, I do believe you, and I believe in you. And no matter how intense your gift may make life sometimes, I want to be a part of it. Charlotte . . . <br>I want you. All of you. The good, the bad, and the ugly. I love you.”<br><br>There will always be a part of me that feels empty. Ike was my twin, and his absence is palpable. I feel it with every breath I take. But I know now I can survive it. And instead of letting the memory of him and the loss of him hinder me, I’ll let it strengthen me.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1521826845i/25262821._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Where one goes</b>…I figured out, it’s not the location we’re looking for, it’s the peace, a solemn place for the living ones that stay behind and even if <b>I don’t know the answer to the question of where one goes…</b> what <b>I DO know is that one NEVER actually leaves. <br><blockquote>They stay IN you forever.</blockquote></b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430656024ra/14741959.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've related two of my very fave songs for each of the characters that carved their way into my heart, <b>Ike and George, and their connection with Charlotte</b> - they are connected but still apart and there’s no way to make them separate on any level other than physical presence…<br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <u>Ike and Char</u>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><b>Although there’s no physical contact between Ike and Charlotte the connection they have makes it even more palpable and painfully sad and the song really says it all transferring the higher meaning of it…the notion of moving on, of realizing the impossible and making it worth it…</b><br><br><b><i>Hold me now</i> by Johnny Logan</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>Don't don't close your heart to how you feel<br>Dream and don't be afraid the dream's not real<br>Close your eyes pretend it's just the two of us again<br>Make believe this moment's here to stay<br><br>Touch touch me the way you used to do<br>I know tonight could be all I'll have with you<br>From now on you'll be with someone else instead of me<br>So tonight let's build this memory for the last time<br><br>Hold me now don't cry don't say a word just<br>Hold me now and <b>I will know though we're apart<br>We'll always be together forever in love<br>What do you say when words are not enough</b><br><br>Time time will be kind once we're apart and<br>Your tears tears will have no place in your heart I wish<br>I I could say how much I'll miss you, when you're gone<br>All my love for you will go on and on and<br><br>Hold me now don't cry don't say a word just<br>Hold me now and try to understand<br>That <b>I hope at last you've found what you've been searching for<br>And though I won't be there anymore I will always love you</b></i>
</blockquote><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Hi0xyltOwc0">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Hi0xy...</a><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392473369ra/8566482.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <u>George and Char</u>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><b>A broken man that hides behind the vices to hide and dull his own pain and shattered soul, who’s not aware of his own life passing by and going to waste…this is the green light, the hope lingering around him, the push so much needed to wake him up, to take the chance in love, to forgive himself and start living again…so, what are you waiting for…wake up and see what's right in front of you...fight for it</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430656024ra/14741960.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>I wanna wake up with you</i> by Boris Gardiner</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>I wanna wake up with you<br>I wanna be there when you open your eyes<br>I want you to be<br>The first thing that I see<br>I wanna wake up with you<br><br>I wanna lay by your side, baby<br>I wanna feel every beat of your heart<br>And throughout the night<br>I wanna hold you tight<br>I wanna wake up with you<br><br>All the love inside me has been sleeping<br>Waiting till the right one came along<br>You can share the love that I've been keeping, baby<br>You can put the music to my song<br><br>I wanna wake up with you<br>I wanna reach out and know that you're there<br>I want you to be<br>The first thing that I see<br>I wanna wake up with you<br><br>And throughout the night<br>I wanna hold you tight<br>I wanna wake up with you...</i>
</blockquote><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=4AuHibzE0aY">www.youtube.com/watch?v=4AuHibzE0aY</a><br><br><br><b>
  <i>One of the best books I’ve read lately or EVER</i>
</b><br><br>For more info and reviews visit<br><a href="http://http//sirensbr.wix.com/sirensbookreviews/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477746456i/20988439._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo IMG_3173_zpserfdzm2a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1233595739" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1233595739" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1233595739?book_show_action=true">Mar 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25007389-where-one-goes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=sweet">sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1233595739" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14789000619839740733"><b>*3.5 stars*</b><br/><br/>This isn't just another romance novel. <i>Where One Goes</i> is an exceptionally beautiful <i>
  <b>love story</b>
</i> that builds a unique world through the elements of love, loss, and healing. <br/><br/><b>Yes</b>, the heroine communicates with the dead -- souls who have yet to cross-over due to "unfinished business"-- but this story has more of a spiritual tone than a supernatural one. <br/><br/><b>Yes</b>, there is a bit of a love triangle, but it's NOT a threat since one of the heroes is ... well, dead. <br/><br/><b>YES</b>, this book sucked me in, </span>
  <span id="freeText14789000619839740733" style="display:none"><b>*3.5 stars*</b><br /><br />This isn't just another romance novel. <i>Where One Goes</i> is an exceptionally beautiful <i>
  <b>love story</b>
</i> that builds a unique world through the elements of love, loss, and healing. <br /><br /><b>Yes</b>, the heroine communicates with the dead -- souls who have yet to cross-over due to "unfinished business"-- but this story has more of a spiritual tone than a supernatural one. <br /><br /><b>Yes</b>, there is a bit of a love triangle, but it's NOT a threat since one of the heroes is ... well, dead. <br /><br /><b>YES</b>, this book sucked me in, held my interest, kept me on my toes, broke my heart and warmed it all at once, then had me reluctant to turn that last page and say goodbye...<b>and I devoured every single bit of it!</b><br /><br /><u>*Full review to follow soon, but here are some things I LOVED*</u><br />- a smart heroine who is just as sassy as she is sweet<br />- 2 super sexy heroes who happen to be twins, but each have a different persona and set of struggles<br />- a perfectly executed, sexy, slow-building romance that was 100% worth the tantalizing wait<br />- adorable jealous moments involving a brooding, broken hero<br />- the many laugh out loud moments that balanced out the tone<br />- family and small town togetherness, which I always love!<br />- a beautifully touching plot that made me feel even after closing the book...</span>
  <a data-text-id="14789000619839740733" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1251514106" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Kathleen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2367556-kathleen"><img alt="Kathleen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451733481p2/2367556.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1251514106?book_show_action=true">Apr 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kathleen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kathleen" href="/user/show/2367556-kathleen">Kathleen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/24323918-where-one-goes">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1251514106" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1448613109035037535"><b>Story Rating ~ 5 EMOTIONALLY BEAUTIFUL STARS! <br/>Hero’s Ratings ~ BOTH, 5 HUGE STARS! <br/>Heroine Rating ~ 5 PRICELESS STARS!<br/>Romance Rating ~ 5 LOVELY STARS!<br/>Heat Level ~ 2 Stars<br/>Ending ~ 5 PERFECT STARS!<br/>Overall Rating ~ 10 STARS! Because 5 is NOT enough!</b><br/><br/>This is not my normal type of read. I usually stay away from emotional reads because quite frankly they ruin me! You know what? This one ruined me and ruined me in the most wonderful of ways. It did not take too long for this book to captivate me and I k</span>
  <span id="freeText1448613109035037535" style="display:none"><b>Story Rating ~ 5 EMOTIONALLY BEAUTIFUL STARS! <br />Hero’s Ratings ~ BOTH, 5 HUGE STARS! <br />Heroine Rating ~ 5 PRICELESS STARS!<br />Romance Rating ~ 5 LOVELY STARS!<br />Heat Level ~ 2 Stars<br />Ending ~ 5 PERFECT STARS!<br />Overall Rating ~ 10 STARS! Because 5 is NOT enough!</b><br /><br />This is not my normal type of read. I usually stay away from emotional reads because quite frankly they ruin me! You know what? This one ruined me and ruined me in the most wonderful of ways. It did not take too long for this book to captivate me and I knew I was reading something special. Never before has a book grabbed my emotions like this one did. It is one of those stories that will stick in my mind for a long time to come. <br /><br />I've read a book or 2 where a character could see or talk to the dead and they did not impress me at all, not true with this one. As a matter of fact, this is my favorite read so far this year and it belongs among my favorite all time reads.<br /><br />Our heroine Charlotte, or Char as she liked to be called, was an AMAZING character. I know this is just a book and she is not real but I LOVED HER! I felt so much for her, for what she had been through and also what she was going through. I loved that she was so strong through so many things. How much she cared for the living and the dead. AMAZING!<br /><br />And Ike OH MY! Yet another FANTASTIC character. He stole my heart right from the beginning and I was heartbroken by the end.<br /><br />Then there was George, Ike’s twin brother. He had many problems but I completely understand why he had those problems. I know from experience what he was going through, losing his brother, then losing himself to drug addiction. I was really happy that he was able to change his ways and I grew to love him too as the story moved along.<br /><br />We also got a whole slew of wonderful secondary characters and then a few that I wanted smack upsides their heads.<br /> <br />There was some good sexual tension added in but the actual heat level was very low, at least for me. Did that fact bother me? NOT AT ALL! The story and the characters were what carried this story, sex was not needed for me to love this book.<br /><br />When it near the end, I was so emotionally wrecked! I’m talking ugly crying, snot running down my face, going through tissue after tissue. It was sad but it was also beautiful all rolled into one.<br />In the end, things worked out perfectly for Char. She was finally happy and she was not alone anymore. She embraced her gift and finally had the love she deserved. <br /><br /><b>I’d like to thank Jen, and all my other friends here at Goodreads for writing such wonderful reviews on this book. Without them I would have missed out on this AMAZING story!</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1448613109035037535" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

At first I was like "Nah this isn't gonna work for me" then I went to "wow, I wonder if this crap really happens" next "my heart breaks for Charlotte for her past and for her present" then "holy shit I'm in love" and yeah you get it, I was all over it. <br><a href="http://s1067.photobucket.com/user/grayanncam/media/Mobile%20Uploads/2016-11/D8AA8A73-D184-4CBD-9477-CA3A94FA5455_zps51d4ah2v.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

She's beautiful, broken, and yet one of the strongest women. I love how she's not scared to express herself and she's willing to willingly hurt herself to do the right thing. But the ending.......<br>My heart just shattered for Ike, completely broke into millions of pieces. Good lord it's still breaking. Let's just say the end of this book broke me and healed me. My only hang up was the timing of the story, just seemed to move so fast, feelings were so fast and instant, but this author makes it all seem so real and believable.               <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14222260-shanny?shelf=favorite">favorite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14222260-shanny?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14222260-shanny?shelf=funny">funny</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1441765057" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15316627691674437946"> <blockquote>
<b>★★★★★ 5 incredible stars ★★★★★</b> </blockquote><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445221144ra/16617249.gif' width='410' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I don't know what to say, I'm such a mess!!! This has been me throughout the whole book!<br/>One second I was<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447593890ra/17025366.gif' width='410' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>And the next<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443559198ra/16376674.gif' width='410' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I was told that this book was going to be emotional but I had no idea it was going to be that emotional!!! <br/>I think I used a whole box of tissues while reading Where One Goes!!<br/><br/><br/><br/><blockquote>
<b> <i>"Go to sleep, baby girl," he whispers.<br/>"Will you be here when I wake?"<br/>His warm eyes meet mine and he smiles softly. "I'll always be with you, Charlotte. Always. Right here." </i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText15316627691674437946" style="display:none"> <blockquote>
<b>★★★★★ 5 incredible stars ★★★★★</b> </blockquote><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445221144ra/16617249.gif" width="410" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't know what to say, I'm such a mess!!! This has been me throughout the whole book!<br>One second I was<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447593890ra/17025366.gif" width="410" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And the next<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443559198ra/16376674.gif" width="410" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was told that this book was going to be emotional but I had no idea it was going to be that emotional!!! <br>I think I used a whole box of tissues while reading Where One Goes!!<br><br><br><br><blockquote>
<b> <i>"Go to sleep, baby girl," he whispers.<br>"Will you be here when I wake?"<br>His warm eyes meet mine and he smiles softly. "I'll always be with you, Charlotte. Always. Right here." And he points to his chest.</i></b> </blockquote><br><br>This is a beautifully written story. It drew me in from the first page and held me there until the very end. <br>You will laugh, you will cry, and you will fall in love with Ike, Charlotte and George. You will feel their happiness and you will feel their pain.<br>The author does an amazing job of capturing all the emotion between the characters. So much so that I felt myself rooting for everyone involved.<br><br><blockquote>
<b> <i>"Broken doesn't mean we're valued any less, it just means we've loved someone so much and so fiercely that losing them feels like we've lost part of ourselves"</i></b> </blockquote><br><br>I have to say a big thank you to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/31719636-snow" rel="nofollow noopener">Snow</a> for pushing me to read this book! <a href="http://www.sherv.net/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="Air Kiss" width="86" height="58" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384733323ra/6943984.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I. LOVED. THIS. BOOK.<br><br><blockquote>
<b> <i>"Moments come and go; quick flickers in time. Yet those moments can have the profoundest impact on our lives. Either we seize them, and wield them to our needs, or we let them go. It's the moments we let go that, I believe, remain with us strongest- because regret is something that never leaves us."</i></b> </blockquote><br><br>If you want a different kind of romance then I definitely recommend this book!<br><br><a href="http://s1083.photobucket.com/user/shanny_i/media/87a20ed7-96d8-4eed-8009-c4681347f304_zpsbblooywv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447592560i/17025180.jpg" alt=" photo 87a20ed7-96d8-4eed-8009-c4681347f304_zpsbblooywv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1178263175" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1178263175" />
    <a title="✿kawehi.reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12789361-kawehi-reviews"><img alt="✿kawehi.reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1425331136p2/12789361.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1178263175?book_show_action=true">Jan 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✿kawehi.reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✿kawehi.reviews" href="/user/show/12789361-kawehi-reviews">✿kawehi.reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/24323918-where-one-goes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12789361-kawehi-reviews?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1178263175" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16959103767324028069">☆ I received an ARC via the author in exchange for an honest review. Thank you! ! ☆ <br/><br/><b>Where does one truly go when they die? Heaven?…Hell?… The in between?... No where? … What happens when you leave with unfinished business and the only person can help you is afraid of their own shadow?.:</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425782631i/13933520._SX540_.jpg' alt='pizap com14257760571321' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425782631i/13933521.png' alt='13671045' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427682342i/14306342._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>There aren’t many books that can actually make me cry but <b>
  <i>Where One Goes</i>
</b> managed to pull a fast one on me. <br/><br/>To state the obvious, this book centers around love, loss, coping with death, and moving forward with </span>
  <span id="freeText16959103767324028069" style="display:none">☆ I received an ARC via the author in exchange for an honest review. Thank you! ! ☆ <br><br><b>Where does one truly go when they die? Heaven?…Hell?… The in between?... No where? … What happens when you leave with unfinished business and the only person can help you is afraid of their own shadow?.:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425782631i/13933520._SX540_.jpg" alt="pizap com14257760571321" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425782631i/13933521.png" alt="13671045" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427682342i/14306342._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There aren’t many books that can actually make me cry but <b>
  <i>Where One Goes</i>
</b> managed to pull a fast one on me. <br><br>To state the obvious, this book centers around love, loss, coping with death, and moving forward with your life.<br><br>Charlotte “Char” is a young women who’ve after one fatal tragedy, developed the ability to see and hear those who have passed away.<br><br>Reeling from the affects it’s forced upon on her, her family, and friends-- Char finds herself floating adrift around the country while trying to grasp and hold on to what normal life she can get while keeping her gift a secret.<br><br>You see, the dead come to her, and with that Char’s [reluctantly] compelled to help them so that they can crossover to the next life.<br><br>That is, until one day she decides to end it all and ends up meeting Ike McDermott--- a strapping soldier who had died in Afghanistan months prior.<br><br>Ike, who’s been in this ghostly limbo ever since his passing, propositions Char if she can save his family, more particularly his twin brother, George, and fellow war buddy from falling apart—then he can help guarantee her a place to live and work and find some sort of normalcy and stability. <br><br>There’s just a few catches that neither Ike, Char, and even George never expected to find--- love.hope.salvation.home.family.healing.<br><br>Now with Char slowly getting to know and falling for these two different guys—one who happens to be dead. The other alive.<br><br>How will everything pan out?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425782631i/13933523.png" alt="quot serif 3 2 orange l" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><b>
  <i>I shouldn’t be reacting this way to him. I’m only meant to help him crossover…I mean, what kind of person develops a crush on a set of brothers, let alone with a dead one in the mix? But I can’t deny I’m drawn to the McDermott twins.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425782631i/13933523.png" alt="quot serif 3 2 orange l" class="gr-hostedUserImg">In George, I recognize myself and my desire to save him has a lot to do with a wanting to save myself.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425782631i/13933523.png" alt="quot serif 3 2 orange l" class="gr-hostedUserImg">In Ike, I see hope. I see that maybe with enough love, being saved is possible.</i>
</b><br><br>How will George and his family react to Char’s gift and her wondrous talent to see and converse with the dead? With Ike? Will Char’s capability prove to be a blessing in disguise? Or will it be her greatest downfall?<br><br>And when that time comes to bid the final goodbye.... can these characters learn to gather what they’ve learned and make the best of what little and precious time we have on this earth? <br><br>Will Ike find the peace and tranquility he’s looking for? Will he be able to let go of the girl he never got to get in life, but in death?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425782631i/13933523.png" alt="quot serif 3 2 orange l" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><b>
  <i>I think this is the worst part, ya know. I can see you, hear you, but I can’t touch you.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425782631i/13933523.png" alt="quot serif 3 2 orange l" class="gr-hostedUserImg">We’ve known it was coming, but even I’m starting to dead the end of this…It will bring me one step closer to having to leave them--- to leaving her.</i>
</b><br><br>Will George be able to let go of his guilt and his inner rage? Will he stop dwindling himself into oblivion and find the absolution he so desperately seeks?<br><br>And lastly, Char. Will Char be able to find freedom, redemption, and acceptance from those around her and her own self? Will she be able to confront her past and accept her gift for what it is?<br><br>Read and you will find out!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427682342i/14306342._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425782631i/13933524.png" alt="11204177" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><b>
  <u>So, my thoughts:</u>
</b><br>To say that I wasn’t affected by this read, I’d be lying, as I would think that at a point of time or two, everyone is affected by the passing of a loved one and experiences the devastation and insurmountable grief that follows.<br><br>What struck so hard about this novel was this quote---<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425782631i/13933523.png" alt="quot serif 3 2 orange l" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><b>
  <i>Suicide is selfish. It’s a complete slap in the face to anyone who has died and wanted to live.</i>
</b><br><br>It’s something so heartbreaking and yet true. To take your own life, you don’t realize the major effect on those you leave behind and it causes for conflicting sentiments of anguish, sadness, anger and desolation. It leaves a deep mark upon your soul.<br><br>Granted, this book revolves around those who had not chosen to leave this world by choice but rather tragically. For me, and my case, where I’d lost my younger brother to suicide, it struck an emotional chord in me deep within my heart.<br><br>I remember on that dark day, I wanted to beg and curse God at why he had to take my brother away? Why did good people have to die? <br><br>What it ultimately made me realize was that in my brother's untimely death, it brought my family together and made me take into value the wonderful family and support system that I do have in my life; and how I could not dwell in the misgivings of the past but move on toward my future.<br><br>It’s like how my sister pointed out to me at one time, “death is so final” and it’s not something you can take back. After all, you only get to live once. <i>Figuratively speaking, that is.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427682342i/14306342._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Where One Goes</i>
</b> was raw, honest, and powerful. Char’s character was so unbelievably strong and courageous throughout as she tries to live her life with this <i>curse</i> as she feels was bestowed upon her. But in the end, she ends up discovering her true calling and potential. And most importantly, how to love her own self.<br><br>I think that’s all you can really do when you’re in this world as we navigate through the highs and the lows and unveil our purpose and why we are here in the first place.<br><br>No one knows exactly when it’s their time to die. We live. And then we die. It’s the cycle of life really. And as hard as it is, we have to make the best out of it and live everyday like it’s our last.<br><br>I really appreciate this read, as EVERY.SINGLE.PART of it made a difference in my life as of now. It wasn’t the type of novel where only a certain part or passage made an impact on me. From the very first time I opened my kindle and began reading it sucked me in and grounded me.<br><br>Thank you Ms. Toler, for in a way, saving ME! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416279206i/11927179.png" alt="Kawehi" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="16959103767324028069" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

</a><br><br><b>TITLE:</b> Where One Goes<br><b>AUTHOR:</b> B.N. I hope it's peaceful and calm. I hope there's water and colour. I hope I'm somewhere that reminds me of all the happy times in my life</i><br><br><b>The brothers are so different, that I find myself drawn to each one for different reasons, one is strong and responsible, the other broken and lost</b><br><br><i>In George I crave his likeness the understanding we share, in Ike I crave his warmth and good heart.</i><br><br><b>I can see you, hear you, but I can't touch you.</b><br></span>
