        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2558835756" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4774659341581218107"><b> <i>"Sometimes I don’t realize how badly I need something until I see someone else with it." </i><br/></b><br/>"Where One Goes" is a very beautiful story of three people but it is not a usual love triangle because one of them is already dead.<br/><br/><b>Charlotte</b> is a girl who looks like Audrey Hepburn. Charlotte is isolated and alone because of her ability to see and talk to the dead. That is why her life is a mess. Even her parents think she is crazy. This happened to her after the accident she had 6 years ago during which he</span>
  <span id="freeText4774659341581218107" style="display:none"><b> <i>"Sometimes I don’t realize how badly I need something until I see someone else with it." </i><br></b><br>"Where One Goes" is a very beautiful story of three people but it is not a usual love triangle because one of them is already dead.<br><br><b>Charlotte</b> is a girl who looks like Audrey Hepburn. Charlotte is isolated and alone because of her ability to see and talk to the dead. That is why her life is a mess. Even her parents think she is crazy. This happened to her after the accident she had 6 years ago during which her brother died. Six years of helping the dead but not being able to live her life starts to feel too much one day and she decides to commit suicide.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480523174i/21320475._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <br>
  <i>"This will never pass. I will always belong to the dead and because of that, I will never truly live. It’s time to just let go."</i>
  <br>
</b><br><b>Ike</b> died 6 months ago but for 6 months, he has been in limbo, not being able to crossover because of the weight of his twin brother who is ruining his own life, not being able to cope with his brother’s untimely death. Ike will not find peace if he cannot save his brother from ruining his life with drugs and alcohol.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Being in limbo sucks. All you do is watch your loved ones suffer and have no ability to help them. My parents seem to be okay, for the most part. My little brother, too. But it’s George I worry about. Most siblings are close, but being twins creates a bond normal siblings could never understand. We’d been best friends since day one. And now, I’m dead."</i>
  <br>
</b><br><b>IKE &amp; CHARLOTTE</b> meet for the first time when he is dead and Charlotte is alive. Just before Charlotte jumps from a bridge to end her miserable life, Ike sees her and tries to stop her but he is hopeless, knowing no one alive can see or hear him. Still, he instinctively runs to her, trying to save her. Surprisingly, she hears him and sees him.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You can see me?” I shake my head in disbelief.<br>She clenches her eyes closed and groans. “You’re dead.” It’s not a question, but more of a statement. The rain stops and silence falls between us.<br>“You can really see me?” I ask again, convinced I’m going mad.<br>“Dead and stupid,” she mumbles. “Obviously I can see and hear you.”</i>
  <br>
</b><br>Charlotte doesn’t want to continue to live her life by helping the dead but Ike persuades her…<br><br><b>
  <i>“Look, I know you’re tired of helping people like me, but I’m different. I want to help you, too. If I can help you, will you help me?”<br>“I guess I don’t have a choice,” she mumbles and shrugs. “You have a deal.”</i>
  <br>
</b><br>Ike and Charlotte are wonderful together. Their banter is so sweet that I wished they had a real chance together.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m not undressing in front of you, soldier boy,” I inform him.<br>“A fallen soldier, dead and in limbo, can’t even get a little peek? That’s just cruel, Charlotte,” he jests, clenching his eyes closed in mock pain.<br>I can’t help laughing a little as I start digging through my bag and warn, “You better not watch me in the shower, either.” He laughs loudly.</i>
  <br>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480523174i/21320476._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <br>
  <i>“I’m going to kill you!” she shouts.<br>“Little late for that, babe,” I reply and jerk my chin. She tosses a pillow at me. It goes right through me and lands on the floor. I yawn. “Ouch.”</i>
  <br>
</b><br>If two of them were alive, they would be soul mates. Even when one is dead and the other is alive, Ike and Charlotte have a special bond and the more they interact, the more they fall for each other hopelessly…<br><br><b>
  <i>"The first time I heard her laugh, I was done. If I were alive, I’d be making a fool of myself to make her mine."</i>
  <br>
</b><br>But because they have no future together, theirs is a painful love no matter how beautiful it is. Still, they try to make the best of their time together. They imagine what their life would be like if they had a chance in this life.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480523174i/21320477._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m sorry I can’t take you in my arms right now and hold you. I’d sell my soul to the devil if I could, Charlotte.” <br>My words cause a sob to break free from her trembling lips. “I know you would,” she whispers as she wipes at her face and nose with shaky fingers.</i>
</b><br><br>***********************************************<br><br>The biggest shock Charlotte lives is when she meets Ike’s brother <b>George</b>. Because Ike has forgotten to mention that his brother George was his twin, Charlotte cannot believe her eyes when she sees the splitting image of the man she fell for "alive and in flesh" because Ike and George really look alike other other than the length of their hair.<br><b>
  <br>
  <i>"I can’t explain what it’s like to see someone dead and see their mirror image in the flesh. My mind is mush right now."</i>
  <br>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480524747i/21320712._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>While trying to help George, she sees how similar and different Ike and George are at the same time.<br><br>George is a suffering man and because of his addiction problems, he is moody. But like with Ike, Charlotte and George also have a sudden and strong attraction to each other.<br><b>
  <br>
  <i>"Our gazes lock for a moment until he jerks away. What the hell was that? Did he just feel that, too?"</i>
  <br>
</b><br>Ike is a beautiful soul, he can make fun of every difficult situation and lighten her mood.<br><b>
  <br>
  <i>“Must be hard having two insanely hot guys around you at once.” <br><br>I roll my eyes at him, but the truth is—it is hard. They’re two identical make-my-tongue-smack-my-brains-out hot guys. But I won’t tell him that. “Yeah. Your looks have me quaking in my boots.” </i>
</b><br><br>***********************************************<br><br>As time passes, things start to get harder and harder for both Ike and Charlotte… And of course for George, as well.<br><br><b>
  <i>Ike: "I’m fighting to give her, and my brother, life, while she’s fighting to help me let go. They’re the two people I love most in the world, and I want them to have each other when I’m gone, but watching it happen is hard."</i>
</b><br><br><em>
  <strong>***</strong>
</em><br><br><em>
  <strong>Charlotte: I’m seriously messed up in the head. I mean, what kind of person develops a crush on a set of brothers, let alone with a dead one in the mix? But I can’t deny I’m drawn to the McDermott twins. In Ike, I crave his warmth and good heart. In George, I crave his likeness, the understanding we share.</strong>
</em><br><br><em>
  <strong>***</strong>
</em><br><br><em>
  <strong>George: "When you told me you loved me the other night, something changed inside me. You marked me, and I’ll never be able to let that go or forget it."</strong>
</em><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480524747i/21320713._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Although it is kind of predictable what will happen in the end, this book is very beautifully written and the story of these three beautiful people is worth reading. It will make you laugh, swoon, sigh and cry. It will make you feel… a lot! It has become one of those unforgettable books for me.<br><br><b>
  <i>Maybe you’re broken, but so am I. Broken doesn’t mean we’re valued any less, it just means we’ve loved someone so much and so fiercely that losing them feels like we’ve lost part of ourselves.</i>
</b><br><br>Highly recommended!<br><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>Additional note after reading it a second time:</b><br><br>When I first read this book 2 years ago, it was a stand-alone book and not a part of a series. <br><br>Later, the writer has decided to add a sequel to it and that's why, I have read this book now a second time to remember all the details. <br><br>And during my second reading, I felt the same. This is an awesome book. Something unique, indeed!<br><br>So, while this book was miraculously good by itself, I have no idea why the writer had to go and write a continuation to it that might probably change everything. <br><br>I have been hesitant to read the new book for a while but then I have decided that I won't be able to sit and ignore it so now I am going to start this new book and hopefully, it will not kill my love for this first book.<br><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>Additional note after I read Book 2:</b><br><br>Unfortunately, I felt the way I feared. I hated Book 2. And I am so angry and so disappointed. <br><br>So my advise for you would be to read only this first book, not the second one where the writer ruins everything and creates an awful mess.</span>

<div id="review_1234380992" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1234380992" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1234380992?book_show_action=true">Mar 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/24323918-where-one-goes">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Jen by: </span>
      Steph Worne
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=buddy-read-with-steph">buddy-read-with-steph</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=damaged-hero-heroine">damaged-hero-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=military-war">military-war</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=new-adult-romance">new-adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=april-2015">april-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1234380992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6159626052384265726">If I could rate this a ten plus stars; I would! This book reminded me again of why I love to read! I think that B.N. Toler did an absolute amazing job of writing a heart felt story that was both heart wrenching and heart warming all at the same time. I was riveted to the page, and nothing in my world mattered while I was plunged into the bittersweet story between a young woman who converses with the dead, and twin brothers; one who is dead and one who is left behind drowning in his grief. <br/><br/>I have</span>
  <span id="freeText6159626052384265726" style="display:none">If I could rate this a ten plus stars; I would! This book reminded me again of why I love to read! I think that B.N. Toler did an absolute amazing job of writing a heart felt story that was both heart wrenching and heart warming all at the same time. I was riveted to the page, and nothing in my world mattered while I was plunged into the bittersweet story between a young woman who converses with the dead, and twin brothers; one who is dead and one who is left behind drowning in his grief. <br /><br />I have to say that while I was reading this story, I was reminded of that lady on TLC; Theresa..who is a lady who speaks to spirits and helps their families come to terms with the death of their loved ones. Charlotte is a young lady who after losing her brother tragically in an accident, started seeing "ghosts" that were unable to cross over to the other side due to the fact that they had unfinished business. Charlotte began helping these ghosts to get their business cleared up so they could cross over to the "other side." The trouble being that while the ghosts were getting their help; Charlotte was being ostracized by everyone including her family. After travelling alone for five years; with the only company being the spirits who need her; she is at her lowest, darkest place in life. She is about to do something disasterous when Ike McDermott enters and basically saves her from herself. They strike up a deal to help one another, and they very quickly develop a very special bond. There is a twist in all of this, and that would be that Ike is dead, and he brings Char to his twin brother George, who is in a major self destructive mode. What happens when Char falls for both brothers?? This is their story..and it is unlike anything you have ever read before! Please don't be deterred from the fact that it sounds like a love triangle, as this is not your typical love triangle that some of us cringe at.<br /><br />The bottom line here is that I adored this story. I rarely push people to read books, as I feel everyone has their own tastes and I hate to lead anyone into something they might not like. This is the one book that I will say; READ IT!!! This is a must read for romance lovers!!! This story, in my opinion is impossible to not like. It is a beautiful story, and the feels that it will give you are enormous! I haven't stopped thinking about this read since I finished, and I just want everyone to share in the good feels that I got out of this book. It has brought passion back into my reading!!! It is ironic too, as I had hesitant to read it, thinking that I might not like it; but I was so wrong. This will be my top book of 2015! I truly don't think another book could come close to making me feel the way I did for the characters in this story. So, I leave you with the idea that you MUST read this and the sooner the better!!! As well, here is one of my favorite lines in the book:<br /><br />"Broken doesn't mean we're valued any less, it just means we've loved someone so much and so fiercely that losing them feels like we've lost part of ourselves."<br /><br />Thank you Steph for Buddy Reading this story with me! It has been a pleasure as usual! I know you are not done yet, and I am going to take great pleasure in experiencing this story some more through your eyes as well!♥</span>
  <a data-text-id="6159626052384265726" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4927413316174029462"><b>4 stars</b><br/><br/>This was a new author to me and surprisingly it was very easy to get into. There was a few things that bugged me like getting George's PoV too late into the story. I felt more of a connection with Ike and Char. The end with Roger was huh???! <br/><br/>I enjoyed this though and not once did I feel bored. The love triangle wasn't really an issue because well one of them is dead. It was kind of sad but there was humour and a great bunch of characters. It's not one I will forget easily. </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1232920191" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5585738667285577505"> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426905889i/14121340._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> 4.5 Stars </b><br/><br/><b>‘This isn’t a life – it’s a nightmare. A never-ending torment of death and servitude. And the pain has become too much to bear.’</b><br/><br/>Wow, this story made us cry and think about many relevant aspects to our own feelings and thoughts on life and death. It was such a beautiful written journey for a variety of reasons. The writing was flawless and the characters had such depth and brought a wide spectrum of emotion. The intense feeling of loss and emotional connection was unquestionable as wa</span>
  <span id="freeText5585738667285577505" style="display:none"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426905889i/14121340._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> 4.5 Stars </b><br><br><b>‘This isn’t a life – it’s a nightmare. A never-ending torment of death and servitude. And the pain has become too much to bear.’</b><br><br>Wow, this story made us cry and think about many relevant aspects to our own feelings and thoughts on life and death. It was such a beautiful written journey for a variety of reasons. The writing was flawless and the characters had such depth and brought a wide spectrum of emotion. The intense feeling of loss and emotional connection was unquestionable as was the message of love and compassion.<br><br><b>‘The wild and beautiful creature may just be the answer. But she needs saving, too, that I can see.’</b><br><br>We were swept away in an unusual romance and found it really difficult to put it down as we needed to know how it was all going to play out. Certain elements were in some ways predictable, however at no stage did those affect our enjoyment. We felt every character; their love and invisible bond and connection.<br><br><b>‘How do I move on without a complete heart? How do I navigate through life with nothing but an empty chest of what-if’s?’</b><br><br>Charlotte was a beautiful heroine who despite her own tragic story brought such hope and closure to others. Her compassionate soul was a ray of light in such darkness and despair. It was riveting to read and we felt her connection to everyone she came across. She also had a feistiness and maturity beyond her years which rationalised situations making her have an ability to stay incredibly strong and focused. To have the capability she embraces after a tragedy which brought her to her knees takes great responsibility. We found it mesmerizing.<br><br><b>‘Sometimes I don’t realize how badly I need something until I see someone else with it. I want to be happy and basking in the glow of early love; that prelude to the delicious things to come.’</b><br><br>Ike and George. We can’t talk about one without the other. Their journey was intrinsically woven into Charlotte’s. Both men had huge hearts and beautiful gentle souls. No wonder Charlotte lost her heart to both for different reasons. They took ours too. Each brought us to tears as we wished for something which could never be. The story went the way it had to and despite the elements it felt so incredibly real and believable. We fell in love with both.<br><br><b>‘I would’ve loved her like she was my last breath. How the hell did we get here?’</b><br><br>Our only real issue is the in depth synopsis; we felt it gave too much away which impacted our enjoyment slightly – it almost came across spoiler-ish. Often less is more, especially when enticing readers to pick up a story. Despite this; we found Where One Goes to be a refreshing, addictive, romantic and tear inducing read which captivated us from start to finish. We HIGHLY recommend this beautiful story by B.N. Toler!<br><br><i>**Reviewed from an ARC copy provided by the author, with thanks**</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409751100i/11016560._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>✦✦✦ TB Blog :<a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">TotallybookedBlog</a><br>✦✦✦ Come say Hi : <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/TotallyBooked/257135974397181%20&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Facebook</a><br>✦✦✦Follow us: <a href="https://twitter.com/TotallyBooked1%20&lt;/b&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Twitter</a><br>✦✦✦Check out: <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/totallybookedb/" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Pinterest</a> <br>✦✦✦ We're on TSU: <a href="https://www.tsu.co/TBBLOG" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on TSU</a></b><br><br><br></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1706993699" />
    <a title="Alice" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21423168-alice"><img alt="Alice" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1440440940p2/21423168.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alice" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alice" href="/user/show/21423168-alice">Alice</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/24323918-where-one-goes">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1706993699" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3478004991361803292"><b> ALL OF THE STARS! </b> <br/><br/><b> Where One Goes was my FAVORITE book of 2016 and it went straight to my list of all-time favorite books.</b> It's a book that I was scared to read, but I'm so glad that I took the courage to do that, because I would have missed one of the best stories ever.<br/><br/>Charlotte has a gift: <b> she can talk to the dead.</b> Yes, you read that right. <br/><blockquote> <i> When the dead appear to me, there’s no weird sound or blurred image. A warning sign of some sort would be lovely, but it’s not a luxury afforded to me</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText3478004991361803292" style="display:none"><b> ALL OF THE STARS! </b> <br /><br /><b> Where One Goes was my FAVORITE book of 2016 and it went straight to my list of all-time favorite books.</b> It's a book that I was scared to read, but I'm so glad that I took the courage to do that, because I would have missed one of the best stories ever.<br /><br />Charlotte has a gift: <b> she can talk to the dead.</b> Yes, you read that right. <br /><blockquote> <i> When the dead appear to me, there’s no weird sound or blurred image. A warning sign of some sort would be lovely, but it’s not a luxury afforded to me. They look like everyone else. It’s only when they see me notice them that I figure out they’re dead. </i> </blockquote><br />Charlotte helps the spirits that are not able to crossover because they have some unfinished business. It all started six years before, and from that moment, <b> she lost control of her life.</b> Everyone thinks she's crazy and she is so desperate that she wants to put an end to her life..<br /><br /><blockquote> <i> But fate is a funny thing. One minute, I’m about to leap to my death, and the next, I’m saved by Ike McDermott. The strong, striking soldier stopped me from putting an end to my despair. He’s the kind of man that smiles and brightens an entire room. <br /><br />Sweet and gentle. <br /><br />He is my savior. <br /><br />And he’s dead. </i> </blockquote><br />I can't really say more because you have to go into this <b> blind. </b> The story is sad and very <b> emotional </b>, but don't let that deter you from reading it. As a matter of fact, this is not a depressing read! It's heartwarming, it will put you a smile on your face in the end and it will give you HOPE.<br /><br /><blockquote> <i> "Would you dance with me if you could?"<br />His brows rise, surprised by my question. Standing, he looks down at me, his expression serious. "Every fucking song. You wouldn't have a chance to dance with anyone else the entire night." </i> </blockquote><br />I'd love to share with you all the quotes I highlightened, but then this would be the LONGEST review ever because I pretty much loved EVERYTHING about this book. And I'm not exaggerating. This author has a gift, her writing is so beautiful and poetic, and every word gave me goosebumps.<br /><br />I've been putting off reading it for over a year because I was scared, I don't deal well with angsty and sad books, but oh boy, I didn't know what I was missing.<br /><br />I have to admit that PNR romance is not really my thing, but this?? <b> This was oustanding. This is one of those books that I want everyone to read.</b> Where One Goes is a book that you absolutely don't want to miss. I know that there are so many books out there and that it's hard to keep up, but I'm begging you, give this story a chance. <br /><br /><b> <u> Like I said, best book of 2016, without a doubt! </u> </b><br /><br /><b> <blockquote> <i> “I love you, too, baby girl,” he whispers. “Here, there, forever.” </i> </blockquote> </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="3478004991361803292" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1799331198" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1799331198" />
    <a title="Hanne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21725822-hanne"><img alt="Hanne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1456934758p2/21725822.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1799331198?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hanne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hanne" href="/user/show/21725822-hanne">Hanne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/24323918-where-one-goes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21725822-hanne?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1799331198" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7027852876398136667">I’ve read 3 other books by this author and I’ve loved them all. They are all amazing and very different. Where One Goes is also amazing and different. I loved this book so much! I rarely read paranormal romances, so I never expected to have a paranormal romance as one of my favorite books ever, but it just happened. I was glued to my tablet after reading the prologue and I couldn’t stop reading. It’s really amazing! It’s an emotional roller coaster and I cried a few times. <br/><br/>Charlotte can see and </span>
  <span id="freeText7027852876398136667" style="display:none">I’ve read 3 other books by this author and I’ve loved them all. They are all amazing and very different. Where One Goes is also amazing and different. I loved this book so much! I rarely read paranormal romances, so I never expected to have a paranormal romance as one of my favorite books ever, but it just happened. I was glued to my tablet after reading the prologue and I couldn’t stop reading. It’s really amazing! It’s an emotional roller coaster and I cried a few times. <br /><br />Charlotte can see and talk to dead people, but she can’t touch them. Some dead people can’t cross over, because something is holding them here. Charlotte helps those people cross over when they find her. Charlotte is lonely, broke and doesn’t have any friends. <br /><br />Ike died a few months ago, but he can’t cross over until his brother is better. On a rainy night, he meets Charlotte. He decides to help her in exchange for her help with his brother. Charlotte needs a change and she trusts Ike. Ike and Charlotte quickly become friends and she helps Ike’s brother.<br /><br />I loved Ike and Charlotte a lot! Ike is perfect. He’s gorgeous, strong, caring and sweet. He’s very nice to Charlotte and wished he met her when he was alive. He falls for her. He dreads saying goodbye to Charlotte, but he knows that he eventually has to. Ike learns her that there are nice people in the world and helps her find a new home. He learns her to live again. I was dreading the moment Ike was going to cross over. I didn’t want to say goodbye to that amazing man! Ike made me cry multiple times.<br /><br />Charlotte is damaged. The last few years were very painful for her and she never expected to ever find a home and love. I felt for her so many times and I wanted her to get her happily ever after! I wanted to know her past. <br /><br />George, Ike’s brother, is hurt and angry. He misses his brother so much. He’s very nice to Charlotte in the beginning, because she’s new in town and she kind of pushes herself into his life. He slowly gets to know her and they become good friends before falling in love.<br /><br />I also have to mention the amazing secondary characters. They made the story complete. Everybody was necessary to the story, but they didn’t took over the story. Everybody was nice and someone Charlotte needs in her life. Charlotte has so many friends at the end of the book and they don’t think she’s crazy.<br /><br />I can’t recommend this book enough! I don’t think my review did this book justice. Everybody should experience this book. Everybody should fall in love with this book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7027852876398136667" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1577242726" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1577242726" />
    <a title="ȷαεlα" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16126654-l"><img alt="ȷαεlα" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589706072p2/16126654.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1577242726?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ȷαεlα" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ȷαεlα" href="/user/show/16126654-l">ȷαεlα</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/24323918-where-one-goes">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1577242726" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2795213251288231828"><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“When you miss me, come here and talk to me. This will always be our place.”<br/>“Will you be here?”<br/>“A part of me will always live here."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Despite its PN features, this book felt very realistic to me. The author has done a great job in including paranormal-cy in a drama book. Maybe there are people who can communicate with the dead out there.Who knows? The world is a strange place...<br/><br/>When I started this book, I couldn't not notice its similarities with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8788554.First_Grave_on_the_Right__Charley_Davidson___1_' title='First Grave on the Right (Charley Davidson, #1) by Darynda Jones' rel='nofollow noopener'>First Grave on the Right</a>. Even heroine'</span>
  <span id="freeText2795213251288231828" style="display:none"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“When you miss me, come here and talk to me. This will always be our place.”<br>“Will you be here?”<br>“A part of me will always live here."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Despite its PN features, this book felt very realistic to me. The author has done a great job in including paranormal-cy in a drama book. Maybe there are people who can communicate with the dead out there.Who knows? The world is a strange place...<br><br>When I started this book, I couldn't not notice its similarities with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8788554.First_Grave_on_the_Right__Charley_Davidson___1_" title="First Grave on the Right (Charley Davidson, #1) by Darynda Jones" rel="nofollow noopener">First Grave on the Right</a>. Even heroine's first name is Charlotte, for God's sake. But I'm glad I read it. It was an interesting book.<br><br><b>Charlotte</b> sees the dead and helps them resolve their unfinished businesses in this world so they are free to let go and go wherever it is that they go. After years of tortures and torments, she can't take it anymore and decides to suicide. <b>Ike</b>, a dead fallen soldier saves her and begs her to save his twin brother's life. She agrees to help him, but when she meets <b>George</b>, she acknowledges that this is going to be a long and hard journey.<br><br>I liked the twins. For different reasons, obviously. <b>Ike</b> is sweet, compassionate and he's just how a perfect bf should be. There's only one thing that is wrong with him. He's dead. I know that his character was supposed to sound not-real, but sometimes, in the chapters told by his POV, he felt like a narrator and very unrealistic. He's supposed to describe what he sees, not what other characters feel. <br><br>I liked <b>George</b> more. After losing his brother, it is understandable that he would want to lose himself anyhow that he could. I get why he did all what he did. All those things felt real. When you can't stand the pain, of course you'll seek ways to dull it. So, when a stranger bursts into your life, with ridiculous claims that she can see and talk to your dead brother, do you just believe her? Don't you question her sanity?<br><br>Our heroine, <b>Char</b> was plain and uninteresting. So annoying. She makes some stupid mistakes and her decisions are often foolish. I couldn't connect with her. She annoyed the shit out of me.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>Why did the word ‘waterproof’ just sound so erotic coming out of his mouth?</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462003140i/18940785.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462003140i/18940786.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There were many things that really were <b>too much</b> for me. <br><br>■ The fact that everyone falls for <b>Char</b> is BS. That is <i>too sweet</i> and not in the good way. I like the existence of anti-heroes and villains.<br><br>■ She plays dumb when she has the attention of the men around her. I don't buy her <i>oblivion</i>.<br><br>■ I believe in the beginning she really wanted to help <b>George</b>, she had a deal with <b>Ike</b>, but after some time, her intentions aren't that unselfish. She really wants to have her way with him. I don't think this is wrong, <b>George</b> is gorgeous (of course!), but her <i>Saint Char</i> behavior gets on my nerves. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ and she's still a virgin. Oh please!) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>■ After numerous of steamy scenes, I really wanted to see her <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[having sex with <b>George</b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Why did the author skip that part? It is unfair. <br><br>Despite everything, the book was emotional. Some parts did really make me cry. Especially when she interprets what the dead want to say to their families or <b>Ike</b>'s desires and longings for the things he can never have. Those moments were really heart-breaking.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>This is only a dream; the two of us imagining what could have been in another time or another life.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>3.6 stars</b><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="2795213251288231828" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1253993234" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1253993234" />
    <a title="-C-" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29144518--c-"><img alt="-C-" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393678895p2/29144518.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1253993234?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="-C-" class="user" itemprop="url" name="-C-" href="/user/show/29144518--c-">-C-</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/24323918-where-one-goes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29144518--c-?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1253993234" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10363827566375993253">Where One Goes is story of love and loss.<br/><i>
  <blockquote> Sometimes that’s all we really have to get us through the hard times. Something as empty and useless as words can be what keeps us treading water in the raging and unforgiving river that is life. And that is exactly what they’ve been for me</blockquote>
</i><br/>Char, a young woman who after experiencing her own tragedy can see dead people. She helps the dead crossover by helping them complete their unfinished business. Her parents don't believe in her. After five years of</span>
  <span id="freeText10363827566375993253" style="display:none">Where One Goes is story of love and loss.<br /><i>
  <blockquote> Sometimes that’s all we really have to get us through the hard times. Something as empty and useless as words can be what keeps us treading water in the raging and unforgiving river that is life. And that is exactly what they’ve been for me</blockquote>
</i><br />Char, a young woman who after experiencing her own tragedy can see dead people. She helps the dead crossover by helping them complete their unfinished business. Her parents don't believe in her. After five years of loneliness, she feels the weight on the shoulders. Char decides to end her life. As she is preparing to jump she meets Ike who saves her. Ike is a ghost and killed in Afghanistan. His unfinished business is saving his twin brother George. They make a deal. They help each other.<br /><i><blockquote> “You people won’t let me be. I can’t even kill myself!” </blockquote> </i><br />Between Char and Ike is a very strong connection. It's beautiful. <br /><i>
  <blockquote> <b>“I love you, too, baby girl,” he whispers. “Here, there, forever.”</b></blockquote>
</i><br />Charlotte develops feelings for both Ike and George and although they are twins, they are very different from each other. Char wants to help Ike crossover but that means never seeing him again and she doesn't know if she can bare the thought of that.<br /><i>
  <blockquote> “How do I save him, and let you go at the same time? How do I do that?”</blockquote>
</i><br />George is spiraling downwards to rock bottom after Ike's death and his pain is still very raw and palpable.<br /><i>
  <blockquote>“Sometimes we have to hit rock bottom before we can make our way back up.” </blockquote>
</i><br />Char and Georg have been through the same things and that make them stonger. The way she challenge him every step of the way is awesome.<br /><i>
  <blockquote> <b>"The good, the bad, and the ugly..." </b></blockquote>
</i> <br />I adored Sniper as a side character. He was humor, sex appeal, and all things fun. <br /><i>
  <blockquote> "If you’re sensitive to sexual harassment, you should probably quit now because if I think you’re sexy, I’m going to tell you."<br />"I’m not overly sensitive, but if you touch me inappropriately, I’ll bust your kneecaps out."<br />"Pretty and violent. I think I just met my soul mate.”</blockquote>
</i><br />It's a very emotional and beutiful journey.<br /><i>
  <blockquote> <b>"I'll love her for both of us." </b></blockquote>
</i> <br /><blockquote> <i> <b>“Broken doesn't mean we're valued any less, it just means we've loved someone so much and so fiercely that losing them feels like we've lost part of ourselves.” </b></i></blockquote> <br />I am not usually read a paranormal romance. I have to say this was first paronomal novel I finish. I read some of the reviews before I read this book and I wanted to give this story a chance. I'm glad I did. I really liked the concept of this book. It is different and wholesome.<br />The show Ghost Whisper kept popping into my head when I read this story.<br />The book is written in dual POV's between Char and Ike.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10363827566375993253" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2234628813" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9094539865131286243">Where One Goes, by B.N. Toler, is a beautiful and unique story!<br/>Six years ago Charlotte (Char) lives through a horrific life-changing event and as a result she can now talk to the dead. They approach her when they are unable to crossover due to unfinished business. Char helps them settle their affairs and after awhile it becomes too much for her. Troubled and ready to give up on life Char meets Ike. He saves her and, in turn, needs her help. <br/>Full of touching and humorous moments this paranormal r</span>
  <span id="freeText9094539865131286243" style="display:none">Where One Goes, by B.N. Toler, is a beautiful and unique story!<br />Six years ago Charlotte (Char) lives through a horrific life-changing event and as a result she can now talk to the dead. They approach her when they are unable to crossover due to unfinished business. Char helps them settle their affairs and after awhile it becomes too much for her. Troubled and ready to give up on life Char meets Ike. He saves her and, in turn, needs her help. <br />Full of touching and humorous moments this paranormal romance is a story of love and loss.</span>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('d2HiaJMMCdNTLxDGGTRq8TcXSSaf2f2nLAkAf9qZiWJE22GVKey4HbkdwS7afiCCK0rl0kld5OfxPIAWRdL01w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('pVmkgJDRG4XT+B7tu0fg6kNdMoHy3PyOTv2s7HDIKEuW4yd9KjGqSznKzwV4DaqZXwCedSRY5c6TyCyF74NV/g==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
